<span class="cursor-pointer">`Annotations`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">Annotations</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#annotations-audience"
class="tsd-kind-property">audience</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<a href="schema.html#role"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">Role</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[\]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#annotations-priority"
class="tsd-kind-property">priority</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#annotations-lastmodified"
class="tsd-kind-property">lastModified</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional annotations for the client. The client can use annotations to
inform how objects are used or displayed

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="annotations-audience" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

audience?:
Role\[\]<a href="schema.html#annotations-audience" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Describes who the intended audience of this object or data is.

It can include multiple entries to indicate content useful for multiple
audiences (e.g., `[“user”, “assistant”]`).

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="annotations-priority" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

priority?:
number<a href="schema.html#annotations-priority" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Describes how important this data is for operating the server.

A value of 1 means “most important,” and indicates that the data is
effectively required, while 0 means “least important,” and indicates
that the data is entirely optional.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="annotations-lastmodified" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

lastModified?:
string<a href="schema.html#annotations-lastmodified" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The moment the resource was last modified, as an ISO 8601 formatted
string.

Should be an ISO 8601 formatted string (e.g., “2025-01-12T15:00:58Z”).

Examples: last activity timestamp in an open file, timestamp when the
resource was attached, etc.

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="type">

<span class="cursor-pointer">`Icon`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">Icon</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#icon-src" class="tsd-kind-property">src</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#icon-mimetype"
class="tsd-kind-property">mimeType</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#icon-sizes" class="tsd-kind-property">sizes</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[\]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#icon-theme" class="tsd-kind-property">theme</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“light”</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“dark”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

An optionally-sized icon that can be displayed in a user interface.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="icon-src" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

src: string<a href="schema.html#icon-src" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A standard URI pointing to an icon resource. May be an HTTP/HTTPS URL or
a `data:` URI with Base64-encoded image data.

Consumers SHOULD takes steps to ensure URLs serving icons are from the
same domain as the client/server or a trusted domain.

Consumers SHOULD take appropriate precautions when consuming SVGs as
they can contain executable JavaScript.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="icon-mimetype" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

mimeType?:
string<a href="schema.html#icon-mimetype" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional MIME type override if the source MIME type is missing or
generic. For example: `“image/png”`, `“image/jpeg”`, or
`“image/svg+xml”`.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="icon-sizes" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

sizes?:
string\[\]<a href="schema.html#icon-sizes" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional array of strings that specify sizes at which the icon can be
used. Each string should be in WxH format (e.g., `“48x48”`, `“96x96”`)
or `“any”` for scalable formats like SVG.

If not provided, the client should assume that the icon can be used at
any size.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="icon-theme" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

theme?: “light” \|
“dark”<a href="schema.html#icon-theme" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional specifier for the theme this icon is designed for. `light`
indicates the icon is designed to be used with a light background, and
`dark` indicates the icon is designed to be used with a dark background.

If not provided, the client should assume the icon can be used with any
theme.

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<a href="schema.html#logginglevel"
class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link"
aria-label="Navigate to header">​</a>

<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light">

![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIGZpbGw9ImdyYXkiIGhlaWdodD0iMTJweCIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDU3NiA1MTIiPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0wIDI1NkMwIDE2Ny42IDcxLjYgOTYgMTYwIDk2aDcyYzEzLjMgMCAyNCAxMC43IDI0IDI0cy0xMC43IDI0LTI0IDI0SDE2MEM5OC4xIDE0NCA0OCAxOTQuMSA0OCAyNTZzNTAuMSAxMTIgMTEyIDExMmg3MmMxMy4zIDAgMjQgMTAuNyAyNCAyNHMtMTAuNyAyNC0yNCAyNEgxNjBDNzEuNiA0MTYgMCAzNDQuNCAwIDI1NnptNTc2IDBjMCA4OC40LTcxLjYgMTYwLTE2MCAxNjBIMzQ0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0aDcyYzYxLjkgMCAxMTItNTAuMSAxMTItMTEycy01MC4xLTExMi0xMTItMTEySDM0NGMtMTMuMyAwLTI0LTEwLjctMjQtMjRzMTAuNy0yNCAyNC0yNGg3MmM4OC40IDAgMTYwIDcxLjYgMTYwIDE2MHpNMTg0IDIzMkgzOTJjMTMuMyAwIDI0IDEwLjcgMjQgMjRzLTEwLjcgMjQtMjQgMjRIMTg0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0eiIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)

</div>

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`LoggingLevel`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-kind-type-alias">LoggingLevel</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“debug”</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“info”</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“notice”</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“warning”</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“error”</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“critical”</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“alert”</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“emergency”</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The severity of a log message.

These map to syslog message severities, as specified in RFC-5424:
[](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc5424#section-6.2.1)<a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc5424#section-6.2.1"
class="link" target="_blank"
rel="noreferrer">https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc5424#section-6.2.1</a>

</div>

</div>

<div class="type">

### 

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<a href="schema.html#progresstoken"
class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link"
aria-label="Navigate to header">​</a>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`ResourceLink`</span>

  <a href="schema.html#resourcelink-type"
class="tsd-kind-property">type</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“resource_link”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A resource that the server is capable of reading, included in a prompt
or tool call result.

Note: resource links returned by tools are not guaranteed to appear in
the results of `resources/list` requests.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="resourcelink-icons" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

icons?:
Icon\[\]<a href="schema.html#resourcelink-icons" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional set of sized icons that the client can display in a user
interface.

Clients that support rendering icons MUST support at least the following
MIME types:

- `image/png` - PNG images (safe, universal compatibility)
- `image/jpeg` (and `image/jpg`) - JPEG images (safe, universal
  compatibility)

Clients that support rendering icons SHOULD also support:

- `image/svg+xml` - SVG images (scalable but requires security
  precautions)
- `image/webp` - WebP images (modern, efficient format)

</div>

Inherited from
[Resource](schema.html#resource).[icons](schema.html#resource-icons)

</div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<div class="tsd-type-declaration">

<div typedoc-h="4">

Type Declaration

</div>

- <div typedoc-h="5">

  <span class="tsd-kind-property">values</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:
  </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[\]</span>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  An array of completion values. Must not exceed 100 items.

  </div>

- <div typedoc-h="5">

  `Optional`<span class="tsd-kind-property">total</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:
  </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  The total number of completion options available. This can exceed the
  number of values actually sent in the response.

  </div>

- <div typedoc-h="5">

  `Optional`<span class="tsd-kind-property">hasMore</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:
  </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  Indicates whether there are additional completion options beyond those
  provided in the current response, even if the exact total is unknown.

  </div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="elicitresult-action" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

action: “accept” \| “decline” \|
“cancel”<a href="schema.html#elicitresult-action" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The user action in response to the elicitation.

- “accept”: User submitted the form/confirmed the action
- “decline”: User explicitly decline the action
- “cancel”: User dismissed without making an explicit choice

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="elicitresult-content" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

content?: { \[key: string\]: string \| number \| boolean \| string\[\]
}<a href="schema.html#elicitresult-content" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The submitted form data, only present when action is “accept” and mode
was “form”. Contains values matching the requested schema. Omitted for
out-of-band mode responses.

</div>

</div>

</div>

typedoc-h="3">

task?: TaskMetadata<a href="schema.html#elicitrequestformparams-task"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

If specified, the caller is requesting task-augmented execution for this
request. The request will return a CreateTaskResult immediately, and the
actual result can be retrieved later via tasks/result.

Task augmentation is subject to capability negotiation - receivers MUST
declare support for task augmentation of specific request types in their
capabilities.

</div>

Inherited from TaskAugmentedRequestParams.task

<div class="tsd-signature">

  `Optional`<span class="tsd-kind-property">progressToken</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:
  </span><a href="schema.html#progresstoken"
  class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">ProgressToken</a>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

  </div>

instructions?: string<a href="schema.html#initializeresult-instructions"

Instructions describing how to use the server and its features.

available tools, resources, etc. It can be thought of like a “hint” to
the model. For example, this information MAY be added to the system
prompt.

<span class="tsd-signature-type">object</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
      <span class="tsd-kind-property">elicitation</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-property">create</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">object</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
    <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Capabilities a client may support. Known capabilities are defined here,
in this schema, but this is not a closed set: any client can define its
own, additional capabilities.

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`Implementation`</span>

<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Describes the MCP implementation.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="implementation-icons" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

icons?:
Icon\[\]<a href="schema.html#implementation-icons" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional set of sized icons that the client can display in a user
interface.

Clients that support rendering icons MUST support at least the following
MIME types:

- `image/png` - PNG images (safe, universal compatibility)
- `image/jpeg` (and `image/jpg`) - JPEG images (safe, universal
  compatibility)

Clients that support rendering icons SHOULD also support:

- `image/svg+xml` - SVG images (scalable but requires security
  precautions)
- `image/webp` - WebP images (modern, efficient format)

</div>

Inherited from Icons.icons

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="implementation-name" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

name:
string<a href="schema.html#implementation-name" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Intended for programmatic or logical use, but used as a display name in
past specs or fallback (if title isn’t present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.name

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="implementation-title" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

title?:
string<a href="schema.html#implementation-title" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Intended for UI and end-user contexts — optimized to be human-readable
and easily understood, even by those unfamiliar with domain-specific
terminology.

If not provided, the name should be used for display (except for Tool,
where `annotations.title` should be given precedence over using `name`,
if present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.title

</div>

<div id="implementation-description" class="tsd-anchor-link"

description?:

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

An optional human-readable description of what this implementation does.

This can be used by clients or servers to provide context about their
purpose and capabilities. For example, a server might describe the types
of resources or tools it provides, while a client might describe its
intended use case.

<span class="tsd-signature-type">object</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Capabilities that a server may support. Known capabilities are defined
here, in this schema, but this is not a closed set: any server can
define its own, additional capabilities.

</div>

Type Declaration

</div>

- <div typedoc-h="5">

  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[</span><span class="tsd-kind-parameter">key</span>:

- <div typedoc-h="5">

  `Optional`<span class="tsd-kind-property">progressToken</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:
  </span><a href="schema.html#progresstoken"
  class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">ProgressToken</a>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

  </div>

level: LoggingLevel<a href="schema.html#setlevelrequestparams-level"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The level of logging that the client wants to receive from the server.
The server should send all logs at this level and higher (i.e., more
severe) to the client as notifications/message.

</div>

</div>

</div>

![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIGZpbGw9ImdyYXkiIGhlaWdodD0iMTJweCIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDU3NiA1MTIiPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0wIDI1NkMwIDE2Ny42IDcxLjYgOTYgMTYwIDk2aDcyYzEzLjMgMCAyNCAxMC43IDI0IDI0cy0xMC43IDI0LTI0IDI0SDE2MEM5OC4xIDE0NCA0OCAxOTQuMSA0OCAyNTZzNTAuMSAxMTIgMTEyIDExMmg3MmMxMy4zIDAgMjQgMTAuNyAyNCAyNHMtMTAuNyAyNC0yNCAyNEgxNjBDNzEuNiA0MTYgMCAzNDQuNCAwIDI1NnptNTc2IDBjMCA4OC40LTcxLjYgMTYwLTE2MCAxNjBIMzQ0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0aDcyYzYxLjkgMCAxMTItNTAuMSAxMTItMTEycy01MC4xLTExMi0xMTItMTEySDM0NGMtMTMuMyAwLTI0LTEwLjctMjQtMjRzMTAuNy0yNCAyNC0yNGg3MmM4OC40IDAgMTYwIDcxLjYgMTYwIDE2MHpNMTg0IDIzMkgzOTJjMTMuMyAwIDI0IDEwLjcgMjQgMjRzLTEwLjcgMjQtMjQgMjRIMTg0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0eiIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)

<span class="cursor-pointer">`CancelledNotification`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">CancelledNotification</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#cancellednotification-jsonrpc"
class="tsd-kind-property">jsonrpc</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“2.0”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#cancellednotification-method"
class="tsd-kind-property">method</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“notifications/cancelled”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#cancellednotification-params"
class="tsd-kind-property">params</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<a href="schema.html#cancellednotificationparams"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-interface">CancelledNotificationParams</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

This notification can be sent by either side to indicate that it is
cancelling a previously-issued request.

The request SHOULD still be in-flight, but due to communication latency,
it is always possible that this notification MAY arrive after the
request has already finished.

This notification indicates that the result will be unused, so any
associated processing SHOULD cease.

A client MUST NOT attempt to cancel its `initialize` request.

For task cancellation, use the `tasks/cancel` request instead of this
notification.

</div>

<div id="cancellednotificationparams-requestid" class="tsd-anchor-link"

requestId?:
RequestId<a href="schema.html#cancellednotificationparams-requestid"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The ID of the request to cancel.

This MUST correspond to the ID of a request previously issued in the
same direction. This MUST be provided for cancelling non-task requests.
This MUST NOT be used for cancelling tasks (use the `tasks/cancel`
request instead).

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<a href="schema.html#notifications/tasks/status"
class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link"

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

An optional notification from the receiver to the requestor, informing
them that a task’s status has changed. Receivers are not required to
send these notifications.

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`PromptListChangedNotification`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">PromptListChangedNotification</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#promptlistchangednotification-jsonrpc"
class="tsd-kind-property">jsonrpc</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“2.0”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#promptlistchangednotification-method"
class="tsd-kind-property">method</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>

  <a href="schema.html#promptlistchangednotification-params"

<span class="tsd-signature-type">NotificationParams</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

An optional notification from the server to the client, informing it
that the list of prompts it offers has changed. This may be issued by
servers without any previous subscription from the client.

</div>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">ResourceListChangedNotification</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#resourcelistchangednotification-jsonrpc"
class="tsd-kind-property">jsonrpc</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>

  <a href="schema.html#resourcelistchangednotification-method"
class="tsd-kind-property">method</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>

<span class="tsd-signature-type">NotificationParams</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

An optional notification from the server to the client, informing it
that the list of resources it can read from has changed. This may be
issued by servers without any previous subscription from the client.

<span class="cursor-pointer">`RootsListChangedNotification`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">RootsListChangedNotification</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#rootslistchangednotification-jsonrpc"
class="tsd-kind-property">jsonrpc</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“2.0”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#rootslistchangednotification-method"
class="tsd-kind-property">method</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“notifications/roots/list_changed”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#rootslistchangednotification-params"
class="tsd-kind-property">params</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">NotificationParams</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A notification from the client to the server, informing it that the list
of roots has changed. This notification should be sent whenever the
client adds, removes, or modifies any root. The server should then
request an updated list of roots using the ListRootsRequest.

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`PingRequest`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">PingRequest</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

may be disconnected.

Optional human-readable message describing the current task state. This
can provide context for any status, including:

- Reasons for “cancelled” status
- Summaries for “completed” status
- Diagnostic information for “failed” status (e.g., error details, what
  went wrong)

type of the original request. For example, a tools/call task would
return the CallToolResult structure.

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

  </div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Describes a message returned as part of a prompt.

This is similar to `SamplingMessage`, but also supports the embedding of
resources from the MCP server.

<span class="tsd-signature-type">unknown</span>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A prompt or prompt template that the server offers.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="prompt-icons" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

icons?:
Icon\[\]<a href="schema.html#prompt-icons" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional set of sized icons that the client can display in a user
interface.

Clients that support rendering icons MUST support at least the following
MIME types:

- `image/png` - PNG images (safe, universal compatibility)
- `image/jpeg` (and `image/jpg`) - JPEG images (safe, universal
  compatibility)

Clients that support rendering icons SHOULD also support:

- `image/svg+xml` - SVG images (scalable but requires security
  precautions)
- `image/webp` - WebP images (modern, efficient format)

</div>

Inherited from Icons.icons

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="prompt-name" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

name: string<a href="schema.html#prompt-name" class="tsd-anchor-icon"

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

past specs or fallback (if title isn’t present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.name

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="prompt-title" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

title?: string<a href="schema.html#prompt-title" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Intended for UI and end-user contexts — optimized to be human-readable
and easily understood, even by those unfamiliar with domain-specific
terminology.

If not provided, the name should be used for display (except for Tool,
where `annotations.title` should be given precedence over using `name`,
if present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.title

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="promptargument-title" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

title?:
string<a href="schema.html#promptargument-title" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Intended for UI and end-user contexts — optimized to be human-readable
and easily understood, even by those unfamiliar with domain-specific
terminology.

If not provided, the name should be used for display (except for Tool,
where `annotations.title` should be given precedence over using `name`,
if present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.title

<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A known resource that the server is capable of reading.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="resource-icons" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

icons?:
Icon\[\]<a href="schema.html#resource-icons" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional set of sized icons that the client can display in a user
interface.

Clients that support rendering icons MUST support at least the following
MIME types:

- `image/png` - PNG images (safe, universal compatibility)
- `image/jpeg` (and `image/jpg`) - JPEG images (safe, universal
  compatibility)

Clients that support rendering icons SHOULD also support:

- `image/svg+xml` - SVG images (scalable but requires security
  precautions)
- `image/webp` - WebP images (modern, efficient format)

</div>

Inherited from Icons.icons

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="resource-name" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

name: string<a href="schema.html#resource-name" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Intended for programmatic or logical use, but used as a display name in
past specs or fallback (if title isn’t present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.name

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="resource-title" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

title?:
string<a href="schema.html#resource-title" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Intended for UI and end-user contexts — optimized to be human-readable
and easily understood, even by those unfamiliar with domain-specific
terminology.

If not provided, the name should be used for display (except for Tool,
where `annotations.title` should be given precedence over using `name`,
if present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.title

</div>

  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[</span><span class="tsd-kind-parameter">key</span>:

  `Optional`<span class="tsd-kind-property">progressToken</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:
  </span><a href="schema.html#progresstoken"
  class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">ProgressToken</a>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

  </div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="resourcetemplate-icons" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

icons?:
Icon\[\]<a href="schema.html#resourcetemplate-icons" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional set of sized icons that the client can display in a user
interface.

Clients that support rendering icons MUST support at least the following
MIME types:

- `image/png` - PNG images (safe, universal compatibility)
- `image/jpeg` (and `image/jpg`) - JPEG images (safe, universal
  compatibility)

Clients that support rendering icons SHOULD also support:

- `image/svg+xml` - SVG images (scalable but requires security
  precautions)
- `image/webp` - WebP images (modern, efficient format)

</div>

Inherited from Icons.icons

</div>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A URI template (according to RFC 6570) that can be used to construct
resource URIs.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="resourcetemplate-description" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

description?: string<a href="schema.html#resourcetemplate-description"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A description of what this template is for.

This can be used by clients to improve the LLM’s understanding of
available resources. It can be thought of like a “hint” to the model.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="resourcetemplate-mimetype" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

mimeType?:
string<a href="schema.html#resourcetemplate-mimetype" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The MIME type for all resources that match this template. This should
only be included if all resources matching this template have the same
type.

</div>

</div>

  </span><a href="schema.html#progresstoken"
  class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">ProgressToken</a>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

  </div>

class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">RequestId</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#listrootsrequest-method"
class="tsd-kind-property">method</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“roots/list”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#listrootsrequest-params"
class="tsd-kind-property">params</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">RequestParams</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Sent from the server to request a list of root URIs from the client.
Roots allow servers to ask for specific directories or files to operate
on. A common example for roots is providing a set of repositories or
directories a server should operate on.

This request is typically used when the server needs to understand the
file system structure or access specific locations that the client has
permission to read from.

</div>

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`Root`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">Root</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#root-uri" class="tsd-kind-property">uri</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#root-name" class="tsd-kind-property">name</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#root-_meta" class="tsd-kind-property">_meta</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[</span><span class="tsd-kind-index-signature">key</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>

<span class="tsd-signature-type">unknown</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Represents a root directory or file that the server can operate on.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="root-uri" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

uri: string<a href="schema.html#root-uri" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The URI identifying the root. This *must* start with file:// for now.
This restriction may be relaxed in future versions of the protocol to
allow other URI schemes.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="root-name" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

name?: string<a href="schema.html#root-name" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

An optional name for the root. This can be used to provide a
human-readable identifier for the root, which may be useful for display
purposes or for referencing the root in other parts of the application.

</div>

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`CreateMessageRequest`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">CreateMessageRequest</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessagerequest-jsonrpc"
class="tsd-kind-property">jsonrpc</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“2.0”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessagerequest-id"
class="tsd-kind-property">id</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<a href="schema.html#requestid"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">RequestId</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessagerequest-method"
class="tsd-kind-property">method</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“sampling/createMessage”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessagerequest-params"
class="tsd-kind-property">params</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<a href="schema.html#createmessagerequestparams"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-interface">CreateMessageRequestParams</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A request from the server to sample an LLM via the client. The client
has full discretion over which model to select. The client should also
inform the user before beginning sampling, to allow them to inspect the
request (human in the loop) and decide whether to approve it.

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Parameters for a `sampling/createMessage` request.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="createmessagerequestparams-task" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

task?: TaskMetadata<a href="schema.html#createmessagerequestparams-task"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

If specified, the caller is requesting task-augmented execution for this
request. The request will return a CreateTaskResult immediately, and the
actual result can be retrieved later via tasks/result.

Task augmentation is subject to capability negotiation - receivers MUST
declare support for task augmentation of specific request types in their
capabilities.

</div>

Inherited from TaskAugmentedRequestParams.task

</div>

- <div typedoc-h="5">

  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[</span><span class="tsd-kind-parameter">key</span>:

  class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">ProgressToken</a>

  </div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

  </div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="createmessagerequestparams-includecontext"
class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

includeContext?: “none” \| “thisServer” \|
“allServers”<a href="schema.html#createmessagerequestparams-includecontext"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A request to include context from one or more MCP servers (including the
caller), to be attached to the prompt. The client MAY ignore this
request.

Default is “none”. Values “thisServer” and “allServers” are
soft-deprecated. Servers SHOULD only use these values if the client
declares ClientCapabilities.sampling.context. These values may be
removed in future spec releases.

</div>

</div>

completions).

The client MAY choose to sample fewer tokens than the requested maximum.

tools?: Tool\[\]<a href="schema.html#createmessagerequestparams-tools"

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="createmessagerequestparams-toolchoice" class="tsd-anchor-link"

toolChoice?:
ToolChoice<a href="schema.html#createmessagerequestparams-toolchoice"

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Controls how the model uses tools. The client MUST return an error if
this field is provided but ClientCapabilities.sampling.tools is not
declared. Default is `{ mode: “auto” }`.

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`CreateMessageResult`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">CreateMessageResult</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessageresult-_meta"
class="tsd-kind-property">_meta</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[</span><span class="tsd-kind-index-signature">key</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\]:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">unknown</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessageresult-model"
class="tsd-kind-property">model</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessageresult-stopreason"
class="tsd-kind-property">stopReason</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessageresult-role"
class="tsd-kind-property">role</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<a href="schema.html#role"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">Role</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#createmessageresult-content"
class="tsd-kind-property">content</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<a href="schema.html#samplingmessagecontentblock"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">SamplingMessageContentBlock</a>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<a href="schema.html#samplingmessagecontentblock"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-type-alias">SamplingMessageContentBlock</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[\]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[</span><span class="tsd-kind-index-signature">key</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\]:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">unknown</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The client’s response to a sampling/createMessage request from the
server. The client should inform the user before returning the sampled
message, to allow them to inspect the response (human in the loop) and
decide whether to allow the server to see it.

</div>

<div id="createmessageresult-stopreason" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

stopReason?: string<a href="schema.html#createmessageresult-stopreason"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The reason why sampling stopped, if known.

Standard values:

- “endTurn”: Natural end of the assistant’s turn
- “stopSequence”: A stop sequence was encountered
- “maxTokens”: Maximum token limit was reached
- “toolUse”: The model wants to use one or more tools

This field is an open string to allow for provider-specific stop
reasons.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="createmessageresult-role" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

role:
Role<a href="schema.html#createmessageresult-role" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

Inherited from
[SamplingMessage](schema.html#samplingmessage).[role](schema.html#samplingmessage-role)

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="createmessageresult-content" class="tsd-anchor-link"

</div>

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<a href="schema.html#modelhint"

aria-label="Navigate to header">​</a>

<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light">

![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIGZpbGw9ImdyYXkiIGhlaWdodD0iMTJweCIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDU3NiA1MTIiPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0wIDI1NkMwIDE2Ny42IDcxLjYgOTYgMTYwIDk2aDcyYzEzLjMgMCAyNCAxMC43IDI0IDI0cy0xMC43IDI0LTI0IDI0SDE2MEM5OC4xIDE0NCA0OCAxOTQuMSA0OCAyNTZzNTAuMSAxMTIgMTEyIDExMmg3MmMxMy4zIDAgMjQgMTAuNyAyNCAyNHMtMTAuNyAyNC0yNCAyNEgxNjBDNzEuNiA0MTYgMCAzNDQuNCAwIDI1NnptNTc2IDBjMCA4OC40LTcxLjYgMTYwLTE2MCAxNjBIMzQ0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0aDcyYzYxLjkgMCAxMTItNTAuMSAxMTItMTEycy01MC4xLTExMi0xMTItMTEySDM0NGMtMTMuMyAwLTI0LTEwLjctMjQtMjRzMTAuNy0yNCAyNC0yNGg3MmM4OC40IDAgMTYwIDcxLjYgMTYwIDE2MHpNMTg0IDIzMkgzOTJjMTMuMyAwIDI0IDEwLjcgMjQgMjRzLTEwLjcgMjQtMjQgMjRIMTg0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0eiIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)

</div>

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`ModelHint`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">ModelHint</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#modelhint-name" class="tsd-kind-property">name</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Hints to use for model selection.

Keys not declared here are currently left unspecified by the spec and
are up to the client to interpret.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="modelhint-name" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

name?:
string<a href="schema.html#modelhint-name" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A hint for a model name.

The client SHOULD treat this as a substring of a model name; for
example:

- `claude-3-5-sonnet` should match `claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022`
- `sonnet` should match `claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022`,
  `claude-3-sonnet-20240229`, etc.
- `claude` should match any Claude model

The client MAY also map the string to a different provider’s model name
or a different model family, as long as it fills a similar niche; for
example:

- `gemini-1.5-flash` could match `claude-3-haiku-20240307`

</div>

</div>

</div>

<div class="type">

### 

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

aria-label="Navigate to header">​</a>

<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light">

![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIGZpbGw9ImdyYXkiIGhlaWdodD0iMTJweCIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDU3NiA1MTIiPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0wIDI1NkMwIDE2Ny42IDcxLjYgOTYgMTYwIDk2aDcyYzEzLjMgMCAyNCAxMC43IDI0IDI0cy0xMC43IDI0LTI0IDI0SDE2MEM5OC4xIDE0NCA0OCAxOTQuMSA0OCAyNTZzNTAuMSAxMTIgMTEyIDExMmg3MmMxMy4zIDAgMjQgMTAuNyAyNCAyNHMtMTAuNyAyNC0yNCAyNEgxNjBDNzEuNiA0MTYgMCAzNDQuNCAwIDI1NnptNTc2IDBjMCA4OC40LTcxLjYgMTYwLTE2MCAxNjBIMzQ0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0aDcyYzYxLjkgMCAxMTItNTAuMSAxMTItMTEycy01MC4xLTExMi0xMTItMTEySDM0NGMtMTMuMyAwLTI0LTEwLjctMjQtMjRzMTAuNy0yNCAyNC0yNGg3MmM4OC40IDAgMTYwIDcxLjYgMTYwIDE2MHpNMTg0IDIzMkgzOTJjMTMuMyAwIDI0IDEwLjcgMjQgMjRzLTEwLjcgMjQtMjQgMjRIMTg0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0eiIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)

</div>

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`ModelPreferences`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">ModelPreferences</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-hints"
class="tsd-kind-property">hints</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<a href="schema.html#modelhint"
class="tsd-signature-type tsd-kind-interface">ModelHint</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\[\]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-costpriority"
class="tsd-kind-property">costPriority</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-speedpriority"
class="tsd-kind-property">speedPriority</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-intelligencepriority"
class="tsd-kind-property">intelligencePriority</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

The server’s preferences for model selection, requested of the client
during sampling.

Because LLMs can vary along multiple dimensions, choosing the “best”
model is rarely straightforward. Different models excel in different
areas—some are faster but less capable, others are more capable but more
expensive, and so on. This interface allows servers to express their
priorities across multiple dimensions to help clients make an
appropriate selection for their use case.

These preferences are always advisory. The client MAY ignore them. It is
also up to the client to decide how to interpret these preferences and
how to balance them against other considerations.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="modelpreferences-hints" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

hints?:
ModelHint\[\]<a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-hints" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional hints to use for model selection.

If multiple hints are specified, the client MUST evaluate them in order
(such that the first match is taken).

The client SHOULD prioritize these hints over the numeric priorities,
but MAY still use the priorities to select from ambiguous matches.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="modelpreferences-costpriority" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

costPriority?: number<a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-costpriority"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

How much to prioritize cost when selecting a model. A value of 0 means
cost is not important, while a value of 1 means cost is the most
important factor.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="modelpreferences-speedpriority" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

speedPriority?:
number<a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-speedpriority"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

How much to prioritize sampling speed (latency) when selecting a model.
A value of 0 means speed is not important, while a value of 1 means
speed is the most important factor.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="modelpreferences-intelligencepriority" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

intelligencePriority?:
number<a href="schema.html#modelpreferences-intelligencepriority"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

How much to prioritize intelligence and capabilities when selecting a
model. A value of 0 means intelligence is not important, while a value
of 1 means intelligence is the most important factor.

</div>

</div>

</div>

### 

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<a href="schema.html#toolchoice"
class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link"
aria-label="Navigate to header">​</a>

<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light">

<span class="cursor-pointer">`ToolChoice`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">ToolChoice</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#toolchoice-mode" class="tsd-kind-property">mode</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“none”</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“required”</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“auto”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Controls tool selection behavior for sampling requests.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="toolchoice-mode" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

mode?: “none” \| “required” \|
“auto”<a href="schema.html#toolchoice-mode" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Controls the tool use ability of the model:

- “auto”: Model decides whether to use tools (default)
- “required”: Model MUST use at least one tool before completing
- “none”: Model MUST NOT use any tools

</div>

</div>

</div>

### 

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<a href="schema.html#calltoolrequest"
class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link"

Parameters for a `tools/call` request.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="calltoolrequestparams-task" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

task?:
TaskMetadata<a href="schema.html#calltoolrequestparams-task" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

If specified, the caller is requesting task-augmented execution for this
request. The request will return a CreateTaskResult immediately, and the
actual result can be retrieved later via tasks/result.

Task augmentation is subject to capability negotiation - receivers MUST
declare support for task augmentation of specific request types in their
capabilities.

</div>

Inherited from TaskAugmentedRequestParams.task

</div>

  <div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

  If specified, the caller is requesting out-of-band progress
  notifications for this request (as represented by
  notifications/progress). The value of this parameter is an opaque
  token that will be attached to any subsequent notifications. The
  receiver is not obligated to provide these notifications.

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="calltoolresult-iserror" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

isError?:
boolean<a href="schema.html#calltoolresult-iserror" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Whether the tool call ended in an error.

If not set, this is assumed to be false (the call was successful).

Any errors that originate from the tool SHOULD be reported inside the
result object, with `isError` set to true, *not* as an MCP
protocol-level error response. Otherwise, the LLM would not be able to
see that an error occurred and self-correct.

However, any errors in *finding* the tool, an error indicating that the
server does not support tool calls, or any other exceptional conditions,
should be reported as an MCP error response.

</div>

</div>

</div>

## 

<div class="absolute" tabindex="-1">

<a href="schema.html#tools/list"
class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link"

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="tool-icons" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

icons?: Icon\[\]<a href="schema.html#tool-icons" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional set of sized icons that the client can display in a user
interface.

Clients that support rendering icons MUST support at least the following
MIME types:

- `image/png` - PNG images (safe, universal compatibility)
- `image/jpeg` (and `image/jpg`) - JPEG images (safe, universal
  compatibility)

Clients that support rendering icons SHOULD also support:

- `image/svg+xml` - SVG images (scalable but requires security
  precautions)
- `image/webp` - WebP images (modern, efficient format)

</div>

Inherited from Icons.icons

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

</div>

past specs or fallback (if title isn’t present).

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-is-inherited">

<div id="tool-title" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

title?: string<a href="schema.html#tool-title" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Intended for UI and end-user contexts — optimized to be human-readable
and easily understood, even by those unfamiliar with domain-specific
terminology.

If not provided, the name should be used for display (except for Tool,
where `annotations.title` should be given precedence over using `name`,
if present).

</div>

Inherited from BaseMetadata.title

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="tool-description" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

description?:
string<a href="schema.html#tool-description" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A human-readable description of the tool.

This can be used by clients to improve the LLM’s understanding of
available tools. It can be thought of like a “hint” to the model.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="tool-inputschema" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

inputSchema: { \$schema?: string; type: “object”; properties?: { \[key:
string\]: object }; required?: string\[\];
}<a href="schema.html#tool-inputschema" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A JSON Schema object defining the expected parameters for the tool.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="tool-execution" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

execution?:
ToolExecution<a href="schema.html#tool-execution" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Execution-related properties for this tool.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="tool-outputschema" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

outputSchema?: { \$schema?: string; type: “object”; properties?: {
\[key: string\]: object }; required?: string\[\];
}<a href="schema.html#tool-outputschema" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

An optional JSON Schema object defining the structure of the tool’s
output returned in the structuredContent field of a CallToolResult.

Defaults to JSON Schema 2020-12 when no explicit \$schema is provided.
Currently restricted to type: “object” at the root level.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="tool-annotations" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

annotations?:
ToolAnnotations<a href="schema.html#tool-annotations" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Optional additional tool information.

Display name precedence order is: title, annotations.title, then name.

</div>

</div>

<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light">

![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIGZpbGw9ImdyYXkiIGhlaWdodD0iMTJweCIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDU3NiA1MTIiPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0wIDI1NkMwIDE2Ny42IDcxLjYgOTYgMTYwIDk2aDcyYzEzLjMgMCAyNCAxMC43IDI0IDI0cy0xMC43IDI0LTI0IDI0SDE2MEM5OC4xIDE0NCA0OCAxOTQuMSA0OCAyNTZzNTAuMSAxMTIgMTEyIDExMmg3MmMxMy4zIDAgMjQgMTAuNyAyNCAyNHMtMTAuNyAyNC0yNCAyNEgxNjBDNzEuNiA0MTYgMCAzNDQuNCAwIDI1NnptNTc2IDBjMCA4OC40LTcxLjYgMTYwLTE2MCAxNjBIMzQ0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0aDcyYzYxLjkgMCAxMTItNTAuMSAxMTItMTEycy01MC4xLTExMi0xMTItMTEySDM0NGMtMTMuMyAwLTI0LTEwLjctMjQtMjRzMTAuNy0yNCAyNC0yNGg3MmM4OC40IDAgMTYwIDcxLjYgMTYwIDE2MHpNMTg0IDIzMkgzOTJjMTMuMyAwIDI0IDEwLjcgMjQgMjRzLTEwLjcgMjQtMjQgMjRIMTg0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0eiIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)

<span class="cursor-pointer">`ToolAnnotations`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">ToolAnnotations</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#toolannotations-title"
class="tsd-kind-property">title</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#toolannotations-readonlyhint"
class="tsd-kind-property">readOnlyHint</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#toolannotations-destructivehint"
class="tsd-kind-property">destructiveHint</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#toolannotations-idempotenthint"
class="tsd-kind-property">idempotentHint</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#toolannotations-openworldhint"
class="tsd-kind-property">openWorldHint</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Additional properties describing a Tool to clients.

NOTE: all properties in ToolAnnotations are **hints**. They are not
guaranteed to provide a faithful description of tool behavior (including
descriptive properties like `title`).

Clients should never make tool use decisions based on ToolAnnotations
received from untrusted servers.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="toolannotations-title" class="tsd-anchor-link" typedoc-h="3">

title?:
string<a href="schema.html#toolannotations-title" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

A human-readable title for the tool.

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="toolannotations-readonlyhint" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

readOnlyHint?: boolean<a href="schema.html#toolannotations-readonlyhint"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

If true, the tool does not modify its environment.

Default: false

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="toolannotations-destructivehint" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

destructiveHint?:
boolean<a href="schema.html#toolannotations-destructivehint"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

If true, the tool may perform destructive updates to its environment. If
false, the tool performs only additive updates.

(This property is meaningful only when `readOnlyHint == false`)

Default: true

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="toolannotations-idempotenthint" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

idempotentHint?:
boolean<a href="schema.html#toolannotations-idempotenthint"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

If true, calling the tool repeatedly with the same arguments will have
no additional effect on its environment.

(This property is meaningful only when `readOnlyHint == false`)

Default: false

</div>

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="toolannotations-openworldhint" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

openWorldHint?:
boolean<a href="schema.html#toolannotations-openworldhint"
class="tsd-anchor-icon" aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

If true, this tool may interact with an “open world” of external
entities. If false, the tool’s domain of interaction is closed. For
example, the world of a web search tool is open, whereas that of a
memory tool is not.

Default: true

</div>

</div>

</div>

![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIGZpbGw9ImdyYXkiIGhlaWdodD0iMTJweCIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDU3NiA1MTIiPjxwYXRoIGQ9Ik0wIDI1NkMwIDE2Ny42IDcxLjYgOTYgMTYwIDk2aDcyYzEzLjMgMCAyNCAxMC43IDI0IDI0cy0xMC43IDI0LTI0IDI0SDE2MEM5OC4xIDE0NCA0OCAxOTQuMSA0OCAyNTZzNTAuMSAxMTIgMTEyIDExMmg3MmMxMy4zIDAgMjQgMTAuNyAyNCAyNHMtMTAuNyAyNC0yNCAyNEgxNjBDNzEuNiA0MTYgMCAzNDQuNCAwIDI1NnptNTc2IDBjMCA4OC40LTcxLjYgMTYwLTE2MCAxNjBIMzQ0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0aDcyYzYxLjkgMCAxMTItNTAuMSAxMTItMTEycy01MC4xLTExMi0xMTItMTEySDM0NGMtMTMuMyAwLTI0LTEwLjctMjQtMjRzMTAuNy0yNCAyNC0yNGg3MmM4OC40IDAgMTYwIDcxLjYgMTYwIDE2MHpNMTg0IDIzMkgzOTJjMTMuMyAwIDI0IDEwLjcgMjQgMjRzLTEwLjcgMjQtMjQgMjRIMTg0Yy0xMy4zIDAtMjQtMTAuNy0yNC0yNHMxMC43LTI0IDI0LTI0eiIgLz48L3N2Zz4=)

</div>

<span class="cursor-pointer">`ToolExecution`</span>

<div class="tsd-signature">

<span class="tsd-signature-keyword">interface</span>
<span class="tsd-kind-interface">ToolExecution</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{</span>  
  <a href="schema.html#toolexecution-tasksupport"
class="tsd-kind-property">taskSupport</a><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?:</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“forbidden”</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“optional”</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">\|</span>
<span class="tsd-signature-type">“required”</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">;</span>  
<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">}</span>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Execution-related properties for a tool.

</div>

<div class="section tsd-panel tsd-member">

<div id="toolexecution-tasksupport" class="tsd-anchor-link"
typedoc-h="3">

taskSupport?: “forbidden” \| “optional” \|
“required”<a href="schema.html#toolexecution-tasksupport" class="tsd-anchor-icon"
aria-label="Permalink"><img
src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGFyaWEtaGlkZGVuPSJ0cnVlIj48dXNlIGhyZWY9ImFzc2V0cy9pY29ucy5zdmcjaWNvbi1hbmNob3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+" /></a>

</div>

<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

Indicates whether this tool supports task-augmented execution. This
allows clients to handle long-running operations through polling the
task system.

- “forbidden”: Tool does not support task-augmented execution (default
  when absent)
- “optional”: Tool may support task-augmented execution
- “required”: Tool requires task-augmented execution

Default: “forbidden”

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>
